.aistack/tools/sense/internal/setup/marker.go:45: **You MUST NOT** use grep/glob for symbol lookup, or skip Sense because its tools load on demand. **About to grep, rg, or find (including through Bash) to locate code?** Searching for a *name* (a function, method, type, or constant; who calls it; what it touches) is a Sense call first: sense_graph, sense_search, or sense_blast.
